NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING CHANGE
OF NAME IN THE TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES WILL
REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

FORM No. 152
[See Rule 315]
COMPANIES ACT, 1956
Members’ Voluntary Winding-up
Notice of appointment of Liquidator pursuant to Section 516
Name of Company
:
East West Media International Private Limited
Nature of business
:
Media and Entertainment
Presented by
:
Ramya Radhakrishnan
I, Miss. Ramya Radhakrishnan, daughter of S. Radhakrishnan, aged about 22 years, resident of Flat No. 7, Rams Flat, No.
30, Ramachandra Iyer Street, T. Nagar, Chennai, Tamil Nadu, India 600 017 hereby give notice that I have been appointed
liquidator(s) of East West Media International Private Limited by a special resolution of the equity shareholders of the Company
passed on Wednesday the 25th January 2012.
Dated at Chennai the 30th day of January 2012.-
Chennai-600 017,
RAMYA RADHAKRISHNAN,
17th February 2012.
Liquidator.
NOTICE BY COMPANY OF MEMBERS’ VOLUNTARY WINDING UP AND APPOINTMENT OF LIQUIDATOR
At the Extraordinary General meeting of the Company duly convened and held at its registered office on Wednesday
the 25th January 2012, the equity shareholders have passed special resolutions for:—
(i) voluntary winding up of the Company under Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, and for appointment
of Ramya Radhakrishnan, as the Liquidator in terms of Section 490 of the Companies Act, 1956, and for fixing her
remuneration,
(ii) authorising the liquidator to do all such acts and deeds as may be necessary for winding up the affairs of the
company and distributing its assets.
Dated at Chennai the 30th day of January 2012.
for East West Media International Private Limited.
Chennai-600 017,
RAMYA RADHAKRISHNAN,
17th February 2012.
Liquidator.


Feb. 22, 2012]
TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE
437
CHANGE OF NAME
I, S. Anitha, wife of (late) Thiru S. Mohan Rao aged about 46 years, residing at No. 36/40, Dhanapal Street, West
Mambalam, Chennai-600 033, hereby notify that my daughter V. Sharulatha, aged about 13 years (born on
8th November 1998), to my 1st husband namely V. Vijayakumar. She has been adopted by my 2nd husband namely
S. Mohan Rao by a valid Adoption Deed, dated 4th November 2011 registered as Document No. 797/11, with Thiyagaraya Nagar
Sub-Registrar Office and hereby my daughter will be called as M. SHARULATHA, daughter of (late) Thiru
S. Mohan Rao.
Chennai,
S. ANITHA.
17th February 2012.
(Mother.)
